NOTES: The next day, Donie Bush announced that he would be a part-owner and manager of the Louisville Colonels in 1939. Red Sox owner Tom Yawkey, and Frank McKinney, president of the Fidelity Trust Co. of Indianapolis and a friend of Bush's, were part of the ownership team. The Colonels would also replace the Millers as the Red Sox top farm team.
